  <h1 style="font-size:24px;font-weight:800;margin-bottom:8px">ForePack Sub Sheet</h1>

  <p style="color:#8B949E;font-size:14px;margin-bottom:28px;line-height:1.7">Add your Supabase credentials to go live. Follow the steps below — it takes about 10 minutes.</p>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#00C9A744">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#00C9A7;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">Step 1 — Create a Supabase Account &amp; Project</div>

    <ol style="font-size:13px;line-height:2.2;padding-left:20px;color:#E6EDF3">

      <li>Go to <a href="https://supabase.com" target="_blank">supabase.com</a> and click <strong>Start your project</strong></li>

      <li>Sign up with GitHub or email</li>

      <li>Click <strong>New project</strong></li>

      <li>Name it <strong>forepack-subsheet</strong>, set a database password, pick a region close to you</li>

      <li>Click <strong>Create new project</strong> and wait about 60 seconds for it to spin up</li>

    </ol>

  </div>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#58A6FF44">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#58A6FF;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">Step 2 — Create the Database Tables</div>

    <ol style="font-size:13px;line-height:2.2;padding-left:20px;color:#E6EDF3;margin-bottom:12px">

      <li>In your Supabase project, click <strong>SQL Editor</strong> in the left sidebar</li>

      <li>Click <strong>New query</strong></li>

      <li>Copy and paste the entire block below into the editor</li>

      <li>Click the green <strong>Run</strong> button</li>

      <li>You should see "Success. No rows returned"</li>

    </ol>

    <pre style="background:#0D0F14;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;font-size:11px;color:#00C9A7;line-height:1.7">create table if not exists fp_bets (

  id text primary key,

  data jsonb not null,

  created_at timestamptz default now()

);

create table if not exists fp_games (

  id text primary key,

  data jsonb not null

);

create table if not exists fp_settings (

  id text primary key default 'main',

  data jsonb not null

);

alter table fp_bets enable row level security;

alter table fp_games enable row level security;

alter table fp_settings enable row level security;

create policy "public read bets" on fp_bets for select using (true);

create policy "public insert bets" on fp_bets for insert with check (true);

create policy "public update bets" on fp_bets for update using (true);

create policy "public delete bets" on fp_bets for delete using (true);

create policy "public read games" on fp_games for select using (true);

create policy "public write games" on fp_games for all using (true);

create policy "public read settings" on fp_settings for select using (true);

create policy "public write settings" on fp_settings for all using (true);</pre>

  </div>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#E3B34144">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#E3B341;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">Step 3 — Copy Your Credentials</div>

    <ol style="font-size:13px;line-height:2.2;padding-left:20px;color:#E6EDF3">

      <li>Click <strong>Project Settings</strong> (gear icon ⚙️ in the left sidebar)</li>

      <li>Click <strong>API</strong> in the submenu</li>

      <li>Under <strong>Project URL</strong> — copy that URL</li>

      <li>Under <strong>Project API keys</strong> — copy the <strong>anon / public</strong> key</li>

    </ol>

  </div>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#9B4DBB44">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#C678DD;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">Step 4 — Paste Credentials Into This File</div>

    <ol style="font-size:13px;line-height:2.2;padding-left:20px;color:#E6EDF3;margin-bottom:12px">

      <li>Open <strong>forepack-subsheet.html</strong> in Notepad (Windows) or TextEdit (Mac)</li>

      <li>Find the section near the top that says <code style="background:#21262D;padding:1px 6px;border-radius:4px">CONFIG — PASTE YOUR SUPABASE CREDENTIALS HERE</code></li>

      <li>Replace <code style="background:#21262D;padding:1px 6px;border-radius:4px">YOUR_SUPABASE_URL</code> with your Project URL</li>

      <li>Replace <code style="background:#21262D;padding:1px 6px;border-radius:4px">YOUR_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY</code> with your anon key</li>

      <li>Save the file</li>

    </ol>

    <div style="background:#0D0F14;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;font-size:12px;font-family:monospace;color:#8B949E;line-height:1.8">

      <div style="color:#8B949E;margin-bottom:4px">// Before:</div>

      <div>const SUPABASE_URL = <span style="color:#F85149">"YOUR_SUPABASE_URL"</span>;</div>

      <div>const SUPABASE_KEY = <span style="color:#F85149">"YOUR_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY"</span>;</div>

      <div style="color:#8B949E;margin-top:10px;margin-bottom:4px">// After:</div>

      <div>const SUPABASE_URL = <span style="color:#2EA043">"https://xyzxyz.supabase.co"</span>;</div>

      <div>const SUPABASE_KEY = <span style="color:#2EA043">"eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6..."</span>;</div>

    </div>

  </div>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#2EA04344">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#2EA043;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">Step 5 — Deploy to Netlify</div>

    <ol style="font-size:13px;line-height:2.2;padding-left:20px;color:#E6EDF3">

      <li>Go to <a href="https://app.netlify.com/drop" target="_blank">app.netlify.com/drop</a></li>

      <li>Drag and drop your saved <strong>forepack-subsheet.html</strong> file onto the page</li>

      <li>Netlify gives you a live URL instantly — share it with your community!</li>

      <li><em>Optional:</em> Click <strong>Site configuration → Change site name</strong> to get a custom URL like <code style="background:#21262D;padding:1px 6px;border-radius:4px">forepack.netlify.app</code></li>

    </ol>

  </div>


  <div class="card" style="border-color:#00C9A744;background:#00C9A708">

    <div style="font-weight:700;color:#00C9A7;font-size:14px;margin-bottom:8px">✅ That's it — you're live!</div>

    <p style="font-size:13px;color:#8B949E;line-height:1.7">All data is saved to your Supabase database in real time. Anyone with your Netlify link can view the dashboard and submit picks. Only people with your Level 2 or Level 3 passwords can edit anything.</p>

  </div>

</div>

</div>

const SUPABASE_URL = "https://wnukobradoupxdjnxens.supabase.co/rest/v1/";

if (!CONFIGURED) {

// ─── STATE ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

let bets = [], games = [], settings = { level2Password:"forepack2026", level3Password:"superforepack2026", dismissedDupes:[] };

// ─── SUPABASE DB LAYER ───────────────────────────────────────────

async function dbGetAll(table) {

  const { data, error } = await sb.from(table).select("*");

  if (error) { console.error("DB read error:", error); return []; }

  return (data || []).map(r => r.data);

}

async function dbUpsert(table, id, data) {

  const { error } = await sb.from(table).upsert({ id: String(id), data });

  if (error) console.error("DB write error:", error);

}

async function dbDelete(table, id) {

  const { error } = await sb.from(table).delete().eq("id", String(id));

  if (error) console.error("DB delete error:", error);

}

async function dbGetOne(table, id) {

  const { data, error } = await sb.from(table).select("*").eq("id", id).maybeSingle();

  if (error) { console.error("DB read error:", error); return null; }

  return data ? data.data : null;

}


async function saveBet(bet) {

  bets = bets.filter(b => b.id !== bet.id); bets.push(bet);

  await dbUpsert("fp_bets", bet.id, bet);

}

async function deleteBetDB(id) {

  bets = bets.filter(b => b.id !== id);

  await dbDelete("fp_bets", id);

}

async function saveGame(game) {

  games = games.filter(g => g.id !== game.id); games.push(game);

  await dbUpsert("fp_games", game.id, game);

}

async function deleteGame(id) {

  games = games.filter(g => g.id !== id);

  await dbDelete("fp_games", id);

}

async function saveSettingsDB() { await dbUpsert("fp_settings", "main", settings); }

async function saveBetsBulk(newBets) {

  bets = newBets;

  // Delete all then reinsert in chunks

  await sb.from("fp_bets").delete().neq("id", "___never___");

  for (let i = 0; i < newBets.length; i += 100) {

    const chunk = newBets.slice(i, i + 100).map(b => ({ id: String(b.id), data: b }));

    await sb.from("fp_bets").insert(chunk);

  }

}


async function initApp() {

  try {

    const [b, g, s] = await Promise.all([

      dbGetAll("fp_bets"),

      dbGetAll("fp_games"),

      dbGetOne("fp_settings", "main")

    ]);

    bets = b || [];

    games = g || [];

    if (s) settings = { ...settings, ...s };

  } catch(e) { console.error("Init error:", e); }

  document.getElementById("loading-screen").style.display = "none";

  document.getElementById("app").style.display = "flex";

  updateHeader();

  renderTab(0);

}


// ─── UTILS ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function toDecimal(raw) {

  const s = String(raw).trim(); if (!s) return "";

  if (/^\d+(\.\d+)?$/.test(s)) { const n = parseFloat(s); if (n >= 1.01) return n.toFixed(2); }

  if (/^[+-]\d+$/.test(s)) { const n = parseInt(s); return n > 0 ? (n/100+1).toFixed(2) : (100/Math.abs(n)+1).toFixed(2); }

  const fm = s.match(/^(\d+)[\/\-](\d+)$/); if (fm) return (parseInt(fm[1])/parseInt(fm[2])+1).toFixed(2);

  return s;

}

function calcPL(grade, odds) {

  const o = parseFloat(odds);

  if (grade === "W") return ((o-1)*10).toFixed(2);

  if (grade === "L") return (-10).toFixed(2);

  if (grade === "D") return (0).toFixed(2);

  return null;

}

function plColor(v) { const n = parseFloat(v); return n > 0 ? "#2EA043" : n < 0 ? "#F85149" : "#E3B341"; }

const gradeColor = { W:"#2EA043", L:"#F85149", D:"#E3B341" };

function badge(color, text) { return `<span class="badge" style="background:${color}22;color:${color};border:1px solid ${color}">${text}</span>`; }

function gradeBadge(g) { if (!g) return badge("#8B949E","TBD"); return badge(gradeColor[g], g==="W"?"WIN":g==="L"?"LOSS":"DRAW"); }

function isL2() { return role === "level2" || role === "level3"; }

function isL3() { return role === "level3"; }

function uid() { return Date.now() + Math.random(); }

function esc(s) { return String(s||"").replace(/&/g,"&amp;").replace(/</g,"&lt;").replace(/"/g,"&quot;"); }


function levenshtein(a, b) {

  const m=a.length, n=b.length;

  const dp=Array.from({length:m+1},(_,i)=>Array.from({length:n+1},(_,j)=>i===0?j:j===0?i:0));

  for(let i=1;i<=m;i++) for(let j=1;j<=n;j++) dp[i][j]=a[i-1]===b[j-1]?dp[i-1][j-1]:1+Math.min(dp[i-1][j],dp[i][j-1],dp[i-1][j-1]);

  return dp[m][n];

}

function findDupes() {

  const names=[...new Set(bets.flatMap(b=>[b.twitch,b.discord].filter(Boolean)))];

  const dupes=[],seen=new Set();

  for(let i=0;i<names.length;i++) for(let j=i+1;j<names.length;j++){

    const a=names[i].toLowerCase(),bN=names[j].toLowerCase();

    const dist=levenshtein(a,bN);

    if(1-dist/Math.max(a.length,bN.length)>=0.75&&dist<=3&&dist>0){

      const key=[names[i],names[j]].sort().join("|");

      if(!seen.has(key)){

        seen.add(key);

        const cA=bets.filter(bt=>bt.twitch===names[i]||bt.discord===names[i]).length;

        const cB=bets.filter(bt=>bt.twitch===names[j]||bt.discord===names[j]).length;

        dupes.push({key,nameA:names[i],nameB:names[j],dist,cA,cB});

      }

    }

  }

  return dupes;

}


// ─── TABS ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function setTab(n) {

  currentTab=n;

  document.querySelectorAll(".tab-content").forEach((el,i)=>el.classList.toggle("active",i===n));

  document.querySelectorAll(".tab-btn").forEach((el,i)=>el.classList.toggle("active",i===n));

  renderTab(n);

}

function renderTab(n) {

  if(n===0)renderSubmit(); if(n===1)renderHistory();

  if(n===2)renderAnalytics(); if(n===3)renderProfiles(); if(n===4)renderUpload();

}


// ─── HEADER ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function updateHeader() {

  const u=bets.filter(b=>!b.grade).length;

  const ub=document.getElementById("ungraded-badge");

  if(u>0&&isL2()){ub.style.display="inline";ub.textContent=`⏳ ${u}`;}else ub.style.display="none";

  document.getElementById("admin-btn").style.display=isL3()?"inline":"none";

  const rb=document.getElementById("role-btn");

  const m={level1:{icon:"👁️",label:"Viewer",c:"#8B949E"},level2:{icon:"✏️",label:"Editor",c:"#00C9A7"},level3:{icon:"🔑",label:"Super Admin",c:"#9B4DBB"}}[role];

  rb.textContent=`${m.icon} ${m.label}`;

  rb.style.cssText=`border-radius:20px;padding:5px 13px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;border:none;background:${m.c}22;color:${m.c}`;

}

function doLogin() {

  const pw=document.getElementById("login-pw").value;

  const err=document.getElementById("login-err");

  if(pw===settings.level3Password){role="level3";closeModal();updateHeader();renderTab(currentTab);return;}

  if(pw===settings.level2Password){role="level2";closeModal();updateHeader();renderTab(currentTab);return;}

  err.textContent="Incorrect password.";err.style.display="block";

}

// ─── AUTOCOMPLETE ────────────────────────────────────────────────

function setupAC(inputId, suggestions) {

  const input=document.getElementById(inputId); if(!input)return;

  const drop=document.getElementById(inputId+"-drop"); if(!drop)return;

  function upd() {

    const val=input.value.toLowerCase();

    const filtered=suggestions.filter(s=>s&&s.toLowerCase().includes(val)&&s!==input.value);

    drop.innerHTML=filtered.slice(0,8).map(s=>`<div class="ac-item" data-val="${esc(s)}">${esc(s)}</div>`).join("");

    drop.classList.toggle("open",filtered.length>0);

  }

  input.addEventListener("input",upd); input.addEventListener("focus",upd);

  drop.addEventListener("mousedown",e=>{const item=e.target.closest(".ac-item");if(!item)return;e.preventDefault();input.value=item.dataset.val;drop.classList.remove("open");});

  document.addEventListener("click",e=>{if(!input.contains(e.target)&&!drop.contains(e.target))drop.classList.remove("open");});

}

function convertOdds(){const el=document.getElementById("sub-odds");if(!el)return;const d=toDecimal(el.value);const msg=document.getElementById("odds-conv");if(d&&d!==el.value){msg.textContent=`→ Converted to ${d}`;msg.style.display="block";}else msg.style.display="none";el.value=d||el.value;}

async function addGame(){const comp=document.getElementById("ng-comp").value.trim(),away=document.getElementById("ng-away").value.trim(),home=document.getElementById("ng-home").value.trim(),time=document.getElementById("ng-time").value.trim();if(!comp||!away||!home||!time)return;await saveGame({id:uid(),competition:comp,away,home,time});renderSubmit();}

function editGame(id){const g=games.find(x=>String(x.id)===id);if(!g)return;showModal(`<div style="font-weight:700;font-size:16px;margin-bottom:14px">Edit Game</div><label class="lbl">Competition</label><input id="eg-comp" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(g.competition)}"/><label class="lbl">Time</label><input id="eg-time" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(g.time)}"/><label class="lbl">Away Team</label><input id="eg-away" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(g.away)}"/><label class="lbl">Home Team</label><input id="eg-home" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:14px" value="${esc(g.home)}"/><div style="display:flex;gap:8px"><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveEditGame('${id}')">Save</button><button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button></div>`);}

async function saveEditGame(id){const g=games.find(x=>String(x.id)===id);if(!g)return;g.competition=document.getElementById("eg-comp").value;g.time=document.getElementById("eg-time").value;g.away=document.getElementById("eg-away").value;g.home=document.getElementById("eg-home").value;await saveGame(g);closeModal();renderSubmit();}

async function submitPick(){

  const twitch=document.getElementById("sub-twitch").value.trim(),gameId=document.getElementById("sub-game").value,betText=document.getElementById("sub-bet").value.trim(),oddsRaw=document.getElementById("sub-odds").value.trim();

  if(!twitch||!gameId||!betText||!oddsRaw)return;

  const game=games.find(g=>String(g.id)===gameId);

  const bet={id:uid(),twitch,discord:document.getElementById("sub-discord").value.trim(),competition:game?.competition||"",away:game?.away||"",home:game?.home||"",gameTime:game?.time||"",bet:betText,odds:toDecimal(oddsRaw)||oddsRaw,grade:null,date:new Date().toISOString()};

  await saveBet(bet);

  ["sub-twitch","sub-discord","sub-bet","sub-odds"].forEach(id=>{const el=document.getElementById(id);if(el)el.value="";});

  document.getElementById("sub-game").value=""; document.getElementById("odds-conv").style.display="none";

  const s=document.getElementById("sub-success");s.style.display="inline";setTimeout(()=>s.style.display="none",3000);

  updateHeader(); if(currentTab===1)renderHistory();

}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// TAB 2 — HISTORY

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

let histFilters={competition:"",team:"",name:"",date:"",grade:""};

let histSort={col:"date",dir:"desc"};

function sortBy(col){histSort.dir=(histSort.col===col&&histSort.dir==="desc")?"asc":"desc";histSort.col=col;renderHistory();}

function sortIcon(col){if(histSort.col!==col)return`<span style="color:#333;margin-left:2px">⇅</span>`;return histSort.dir==="asc"?`<span style="color:#00C9A7;margin-left:2px">↑</span>`:`<span style="color:#00C9A7;margin-left:2px">↓</span>`;}

function renderHistory(){

  const f=histFilters;

  let fl=[...bets].filter(b=>{

    if(f.competition&&!b.competition?.toLowerCase().includes(f.competition.toLowerCase()))return false;

    if(f.team&&![b.away,b.home].join(" ").toLowerCase().includes(f.team.toLowerCase()))return false;

    if(f.name&&![b.twitch,b.discord].join(" ").toLowerCase().includes(f.name.toLowerCase()))return false;

    if(f.date&&!b.date?.startsWith(f.date))return false;

    if(f.grade==="TBD"&&b.grade)return false;

    if(f.grade&&f.grade!=="TBD"&&b.grade!==f.grade)return false;

    return true;

  });

  const dir=histSort.dir==="asc"?1:-1;

  fl.sort((a,b)=>{

    if(histSort.col==="date")return dir*(new Date(a.date)-new Date(b.date));

    if(histSort.col==="odds")return dir*(parseFloat(a.odds||0)-parseFloat(b.odds||0));

    if(histSort.col==="pl")return dir*(parseFloat(calcPL(a.grade,a.odds)||"-999")-parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||"-999"));

    if(histSort.col==="grade"){const o={W:0,D:1,L:2};return dir*((o[a.grade]??3)-(o[b.grade]??3));}

    return dir*(new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date));

  });

  const gf=fl.filter(b=>b.grade);

  const fW=gf.filter(b=>b.grade==="W").length,fL=gf.filter(b=>b.grade==="L").length;

  const fPL=gf.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0),0);

  const th=`padding:9px 8px;text-align:left;color:#8B949E;font-weight:700;font-size:10px;letter-spacing:1px;text-transform:uppercase;white-space:nowrap;background:#0D0F14`;

  const ths=th+`;cursor:pointer;user-select:none`;

  const rows=fl.length===0?`<tr><td colspan="${isL2()?10:8}" style="padding:22px;text-align:center;color:#8B949E">No bets found</td></tr>`:fl.map(b=>{

    const pl=calcPL(b.grade,b.odds);

    return`<tr>

      ${isL2()?`<td><div style="display:flex;gap:2px">${["W","L","D"].map(g=>`<button class="grade-btn ${b.grade===g?"active-"+g:""}" onclick="gradebet('${b.id}','${g}')">${g}</button>`).join("")}</div></td>`:""}

      <td>${gradeBadge(b.grade)}</td>

      <td style="color:#8B949E;white-space:nowrap">${new Date(b.date).toLocaleDateString()}</td>

      <td style="color:#00C9A7;font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap">${esc(b.twitch)}</td>

      <td style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px;white-space:nowrap">${esc(b.discord)||"—"}</td>

      <td style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:11px">${esc(b.away)} vs ${esc(b.home)}</td>

      <td style="max-width:160px;font-size:11px">${esc(b.bet)}</td>

      <td style="font-family:monospace;font-weight:700">${esc(b.odds)}</td>

      <td style="font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;color:${pl===null?"#8B949E":plColor(pl)}">${pl===null?"—":`${parseFloat(pl)>=0?"+":""}$${pl}`}</td>

      ${isL2()?`<td><div style="display:flex;gap:3px">

        <button style="background:#58A6FF22;border:1px solid #58A6FF55;color:#58A6FF;border-radius:5px;padding:2px 7px;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;font-weight:700" onclick="editBet('${b.id}')">Edit</button>

        ${isL3()?`<button style="background:#F8514922;border:1px solid #F8514955;color:#F85149;border-radius:5px;padding:2px 7px;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;font-weight:700" onclick="delBet('${b.id}')">Del</button>`:""}

      </div></td>`:""}

    </tr>`;}).join("");

  document.getElementById("tab-1").innerHTML=`<div class="page">

    <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:12px;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:7px">

      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px">📊 History (${fl.length})</div>

      <div style="display:flex;gap:7px;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap">

        ${gf.length?`<span style="font-size:12px;color:#8B949E">${fW}W/${fL}L · <span style="color:${plColor(fPL)};font-weight:700">${fPL>=0?"+":""}$${fPL.toFixed(2)}</span></span>`:""}

        <span style="background:#E3B34122;border:1px solid #E3B34155;color:#E3B341;border-radius:20px;padding:2px 10px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700">⏳ ${bets.filter(b=>!b.grade).length} ungraded</span>

      </div>

    </div>

    <div class="card" style="padding:10px;margin-bottom:10px">

      <div class="grid2" style="gap:7px;margin-bottom:7px">

        <input class="inp" style="font-size:12px" placeholder="Filter: Competition" value="${esc(f.competition)}" oninput="histFilters.competition=this.value;renderHistory()"/>

        <input class="inp" style="font-size:12px" placeholder="Filter: Team" value="${esc(f.team)}" oninput="histFilters.team=this.value;renderHistory()"/>

        <input class="inp" style="font-size:12px" placeholder="Filter: Name" value="${esc(f.name)}" oninput="histFilters.name=this.value;renderHistory()"/>

        <input class="inp" style="font-size:12px" placeholder="Filter: Date (YYYY-MM-DD)" value="${esc(f.date)}" oninput="histFilters.date=this.value;renderHistory()"/>

      </div>

      <div style="display:flex;gap:5px;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:center">

        <span style="font-size:10px;color:#8B949E;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px">Show:</span>

        ${[["","Everyone"],["W","✅ Winners"],["L","❌ Losers"],["D","🟡 Draws"],["TBD","⏳ Ungraded"]].map(([val,lbl])=>`<button onclick="histFilters.grade='${val}';renderHistory()" style="padding:4px 10px;border-radius:20px;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;border:none;background:${f.grade===val?"#00C9A7":"#21262D"};color:${f.grade===val?"#0D0F14":"#8B949E"}">${lbl}</button>`).join("")}

      </div>

    </div>

    <div style="overflow-x:auto;border-radius:12px;border:1px solid #21262D">

      <table><thead><tr>

        ${isL2()?`<th style="${th}">Grade</th>`:""}

        <th style="${ths}" onclick="sortBy('grade')">Result ${sortIcon("grade")}</th>

        <th style="${ths}" onclick="sortBy('date')">Date ${sortIcon("date")}</th>

        <th style="${th}">Twitch</th><th style="${th}">Discord</th><th style="${th}">Match</th><th style="${th}">Bet</th>

        <th style="${ths}" onclick="sortBy('odds')">Odds ${sortIcon("odds")}</th>

        <th style="${ths}" onclick="sortBy('pl')">P/L ${sortIcon("pl")}</th>

        ${isL2()?`<th style="${th}">Actions</th>`:""}

      </tr></thead><tbody>${rows}</tbody></table>

    </div></div>`;

}

async function gradebet(id,grade){const bet=bets.find(b=>String(b.id)===id);if(!bet)return;bet.grade=bet.grade===grade?null:grade;await saveBet(bet);updateHeader();renderHistory();}

function editBet(id){

  const b=bets.find(x=>String(x.id)===id);if(!b)return;

  showModal(`<div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:4px">✏️ Edit Pick</div>

    <div style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E;margin-bottom:14px">Changes save immediately to the database.</div>

    <label class="lbl">Twitch Name</label><input id="eb-twitch" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(b.twitch)}"/>

    <label class="lbl">Discord Name</label><input id="eb-discord" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(b.discord||"")}"/>

    <label class="lbl">Match</label><div class="grid2" style="margin-bottom:8px"><input id="eb-away" class="inp" placeholder="Away" value="${esc(b.away||"")}"/><input id="eb-home" class="inp" placeholder="Home" value="${esc(b.home||"")}"/></div>

    <label class="lbl">Competition</label><input id="eb-comp" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(b.competition||"")}"/>

    <label class="lbl">Bet</label><input id="eb-bet" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(b.bet||"")}"/>

    <label class="lbl">Odds</label><input id="eb-odds" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:8px" value="${esc(b.odds||"")}" onblur="const d=toDecimal(this.value);if(d&&d!==this.value)this.value=d"/>

    <label class="lbl">Grade</label>

    <select id="eb-grade" class="inp" style="margin-bottom:14px">

      <option value="" ${!b.grade?"selected":""}>— Ungraded —</option>

      <option value="W" ${b.grade==="W"?"selected":""}>W — Win</option>

      <option value="L" ${b.grade==="L"?"selected":""}>L — Loss</option>

      <option value="D" ${b.grade==="D"?"selected":""}>D — Draw</option>

    </select>

    <div style="display:flex;gap:8px"><button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="saveEditBet('${id}')">Save Changes</button><button class="btn btn-ghost" onclick="closeModal()">Cancel</button></div>`,500);

}

async function saveEditBet(id){

  const b=bets.find(x=>String(x.id)===id);if(!b)return;

  b.twitch=document.getElementById("eb-twitch").value.trim();b.discord=document.getElementById("eb-discord").value.trim();

  b.away=document.getElementById("eb-away").value.trim();b.home=document.getElementById("eb-home").value.trim();

  b.competition=document.getElementById("eb-comp").value.trim();b.bet=document.getElementById("eb-bet").value.trim();

  b.odds=toDecimal(document.getElementById("eb-odds").value.trim())||document.getElementById("eb-odds").value.trim();

  b.grade=document.getElementById("eb-grade").value||null;

  await saveBet(b);closeModal();updateHeader();renderHistory();if(currentTab===2)renderAnalytics();

}

async function delBet(id){if(!confirm("Delete this pick permanently?"))return;await deleteBetDB(parseFloat(id));updateHeader();renderHistory();}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// TAB 3 — ANALYTICS

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

let analyticsDay="";

function renderAnalytics(){

  const graded=bets.filter(b=>b.grade);

  const today=new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];

  const dayBets=graded.filter(b=>b.date?.startsWith(analyticsDay||today));

  const byP={};graded.forEach(b=>{const k=b.twitch||b.discord||"Unknown";if(!byP[k])byP[k]={name:k,W:0,L:0,D:0,bets:[]};byP[k][b.grade]++;byP[k].bets.push(b);});

  const people=Object.values(byP).map(p=>{const tot=p.W+p.L+p.D;const pl=p.bets.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0),0);return{...p,tot,pl:pl.toFixed(2),wr:tot?((p.W/tot)*100).toFixed(1):0};});

  const byC={};graded.forEach(b=>{if(!byC[b.competition])byC[b.competition]={name:b.competition,pl:0,W:0,L:0,D:0,count:0};byC[b.competition].pl+=parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0);byC[b.competition][b.grade]++;byC[b.competition].count++;});

  const comps=Object.values(byC).sort((a,b)=>b.pl-a.pl);

  const totW=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="W").length,totL=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="L").length,totD=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="D").length;

  const totPL=graded.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0),0);

  const totWR=graded.length?((totW/graded.length)*100).toFixed(1):0;

  const dayW=dayBets.filter(b=>b.grade==="W").length,dayL=dayBets.filter(b=>b.grade==="L").length;

  const dayPL=dayBets.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0),0);

  const top10WR=[...people].sort((a,b)=>parseFloat(b.wr)-parseFloat(a.wr)).slice(0,10);

  const top10PL=[...people].sort((a,b)=>parseFloat(b.pl)-parseFloat(a.pl)).slice(0,10);

  const mostActive=[...people].sort((a,b)=>b.tot-a.tot).slice(0,5);

  const avgOdds=graded.length?(graded.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(b.odds||1),0)/graded.length).toFixed(2):"—";

  const bigWin=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="W").sort((a,b)=>parseFloat(b.odds)-parseFloat(a.odds))[0];

  const streak=(()=>{const s=[...graded].sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date));let c=0;for(const b of s){if(b.grade==="W")c++;else break;}return c;})();

  function sc(val,lbl,color="#E6EDF3"){return`<div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val" style="color:${color}">${val}</div><div class="stat-lbl">${lbl}</div></div>`;}

  function lb(title,data,vFn,cFn){return`<div class="card"><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:10px">${title}</div>${data.length===0?`<div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px">No graded bets yet</div>`:data.map((p,i)=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #21262D"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:7px"><span style="color:${i<3?"#E3B341":"#8B949E"};font-weight:800;min-width:18px;font-size:11px">#${i+1}</span><span style="color:#00C9A7;font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${esc(p.name)}</span></div><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px"><span style="color:#8B949E;font-size:10px">${p.W}W/${p.L}L/${p.D}D</span><span style="font-weight:700;font-size:12px;color:${cFn(p)}">${vFn(p)}</span></div></div>`).join("")}</div>`;}

  const allDupes=findDupes(),dismissed=settings.dismissedDupes||[];

  const activeDupes=allDupes.filter(d=>!dismissed.includes(d.key));

  const dupeHtml=activeDupes.length===0?"":(`<div class="card" style="border-color:#E3B34144;background:#E3B34108"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:7px;margin-bottom:10px"><span style="font-size:15px">🔍</span><div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:#E3B341">Profile Integrity Alerts</div><div style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E;margin-top:1px">${activeDupes.length} possible duplicate${activeDupes.length!==1?"s":""}${isL2()?" — check box to dismiss":""}</div></div></div><div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:7px">${activeDupes.map(d=>`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;background:#0D0F14;border-radius:8px;padding:9px 12px;gap:10px"><div style="flex:1"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap"><span style="font-weight:700;color:#00C9A7;font-size:12px">${esc(d.nameA)}</span><span style="color:#8B949E;font-size:10px">(${d.cA})</span><span style="color:#E3B341">≈</span><span style="font-weight:700;color:#00C9A7;font-size:12px">${esc(d.nameB)}</span><span style="color:#8B949E;font-size:10px">(${d.cB})</span></div><div style="font-size:10px;color:#8B949E;margin-top:2px">${d.dist} char${d.dist!==1?"s":""} apart</div></div>${isL2()?`<label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;cursor:pointer;white-space:nowrap"><input type="checkbox" onchange="dismissDupe('${esc(d.key)}')" style="width:15px;height:15px;cursor:pointer;accent-color:#00C9A7"/><span style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E">Resolved</span></label>`:""}</div>`).join("")}</div></div>`);

  document.getElementById("tab-2").innerHTML=`<div class="page">

    <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">📈 Analytics</div>

    ${dupeHtml}

    <div class="stats-row">${sc(graded.length,"Graded Bets")}${sc(totWR+"%","Win Rate","#00C9A7")}${sc(`${totW}W/${totL}L/${totD}D`,"Record")}${sc(`${totPL>=0?"+":""}$${totPL.toFixed(2)}`,"Total P/L",plColor(totPL))}${sc(streak,"Streak","#E3B341")}</div>

    <div class="card">

      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:10px">

        <span style="font-weight:700;font-size:12px">📅 Day Stats</span>

        <input type="date" class="inp" style="width:160px;font-size:12px" value="${analyticsDay}" onchange="analyticsDay=this.value;renderAnalytics()"/>

        ${analyticsDay?`<button class="btn btn-ghost" style="padding:5px 10px;font-size:11px" onclick="analyticsDay='';renderAnalytics()">Today</button>`:""}

      </div>

      <div class="stats-row">${sc(dayBets.length,"Bets")}${sc(`${dayW}W/${dayL}L`,"Record")}${sc(dayBets.length?((dayW/dayBets.length)*100).toFixed(1)+"%":"0%","Win Rate","#00C9A7")}${sc(`${dayPL>=0?"+":""}$${dayPL.toFixed(2)}`,"P/L",plColor(dayPL))}</div>

    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:12px">

      ${lb("🏆 Top 10 — Win Rate",top10WR,p=>`${p.wr}%`,()=>"#2EA043")}

      ${lb("💰 Top 10 — Profit/Loss",top10PL,p=>`${parseFloat(p.pl)>=0?"+":""}$${p.pl}`,p=>plColor(p.pl))}

    </div>

    <div class="card">

      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:10px">🏟️ Competition Profitability</div>

      ${comps.length===0?`<div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px">No data yet</div>`:comps.map(c=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #21262D"><div>${badge("#58A6FF",c.name)}<span style="color:#8B949E;font-size:10px;margin-left:7px">${c.count} bets · ${c.W}W/${c.L}L/${c.D}D</span></div><span style="font-weight:700;color:${plColor(c.pl)}">${c.pl>=0?"+":""}$${c.pl.toFixed(2)}</span></div>`).join("")}

    </div>

    <div class="stats-row">${sc(avgOdds==="—"?"—":avgOdds+"x","Avg Odds","#58A6FF")}${sc(bigWin?bigWin.odds+"x":"—","Biggest Win","#E3B341")}${sc(comps[0]?.name||"—","Top Comp","#00C9A7")}${sc(Object.keys(byP).length,"Unique Bettors")}</div>

    <div class="card">

      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:10px">🎯 Most Active Bettors</div>

      ${mostActive.length===0?`<div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px">No data yet</div>`:mostActive.map(p=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #21262D"><span style="color:#00C9A7;font-weight:600;font-size:12px">${esc(p.name)}</span><span style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px">${p.tot} picks</span></div>`).join("")}

    </div></div>`;

}

async function dismissDupe(key){if(!settings.dismissedDupes)settings.dismissedDupes=[];settings.dismissedDupes.push(key);await saveSettingsDB();renderAnalytics();}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// TAB 4 — PROFILES

// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

function renderProfiles(){

  const allNames=[...new Set(bets.flatMap(b=>[b.twitch,b.discord].filter(Boolean)))];

  document.getElementById("tab-3").innerHTML=`<div class="page">

    <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:12px">👤 Bettor Profiles</div>

    <div class="card" style="padding:10px">

      <div style="display:flex;gap:8px">

        <div class="ac-wrap" style="flex:1"><input id="prof-search" class="inp" placeholder="Search Twitch or Discord name…" onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')searchProfile()"/><div id="prof-search-drop" class="ac-drop"></div></div>

        <button class="btn btn-primary" onclick="searchProfile()">Search</button>

      </div>

    </div>

    <div id="profile-result"></div></div>`;

  setupAC("prof-search",allNames);

}

function searchProfile(){

  const term=document.getElementById("prof-search")?.value.trim().toLowerCase();if(!term)return;

  const ub=bets.filter(b=>(b.twitch&&b.twitch.toLowerCase()===term)||(b.discord&&b.discord.toLowerCase()===term));

  const el=document.getElementById("profile-result");

  if(!ub.length){el.innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="text-align:center;color:#8B949E;padding:28px">No bettor found.</div>`;return;}

  const name=ub[0].twitch||ub[0].discord;

  const graded=ub.filter(b=>b.grade);

  const W=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="W").length,L=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="L").length,D=graded.filter(b=>b.grade==="D").length;

  const pl=graded.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0),0);

  const avgOdds=graded.length?(graded.reduce((s,b)=>s+parseFloat(b.odds||1),0)/graded.length).toFixed(2):0;

  const winRate=graded.length?((W/graded.length)*100).toFixed(1):0;

  const byC={};graded.forEach(b=>{if(!byC[b.competition])byC[b.competition]={pl:0,count:0};byC[b.competition].pl+=parseFloat(calcPL(b.grade,b.odds)||0);byC[b.competition].count++;});

  const bestComp=Object.entries(byC).sort((a,b)=>b[1].pl-a[1].pl)[0];

  const streak=(()=>{const s=[...graded].sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date));let c=0;for(const b of s){if(b.grade==="W")c++;else break;}return c;})();

  window._profileBlurb={name,W,L,D,wr:winRate,pl:pl.toFixed(2),odds:avgOdds,streak,total:ub.length,graded:graded.length};

  const recentRows=[...ub].sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date)).slice(0,15).map(b=>{const p=calcPL(b.grade,b.odds);return`<tr><td style="color:#8B949E;white-space:nowrap">${new Date(b.date).toLocaleDateString()}</td><td style="white-space:nowrap;font-size:11px">${esc(b.away)} vs ${esc(b.home)}</td><td style="font-size:11px">${esc(b.bet)}</td><td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:11px">${esc(b.odds)}</td><td>${gradeBadge(b.grade)}</td><td style="font-weight:700;white-space:nowrap;color:${p===null?"#8B949E":plColor(p)}">${p===null?"—":`${parseFloat(p)>=0?"+":""}$${p}`}</td></tr>`;}).join("");

  el.innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="border:1px solid #00C9A744">

    <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;margin-bottom:14px">

      <div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:#00C9A7">${esc(name)}</div><div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px;margin-top:2px">${ub.length} picks · ${graded.length} graded</div></div>

      <button class="btn btn-ghost" id="blurb-btn" style="font-size:12px" onclick="genBlurb()">✨ AI Blurb</button>

    </div>

    <div id="blurb-box" style="display:none;background:#00C9A711;border:1px solid #00C9A733;border-radius:10px;padding:12px;margin-bottom:14px;font-style:italic;line-height:1.6;font-size:12px"></div>

    <div class="stats-row">

      <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val" style="color:#00C9A7">${winRate}%</div><div class="stat-lbl">Win Rate</div></div>

      <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val">${W}W/${L}L/${D}D</div><div class="stat-lbl">Record</div></div>

      <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val" style="color:${plColor(pl)}">${pl>=0?"+":""}$${pl.toFixed(2)}</div><div class="stat-lbl">P/L</div></div>

      <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val">${avgOdds}x</div><div class="stat-lbl">Avg Odds</div></div>

      <div class="stat-card"><div class="stat-val" style="color:#E3B341">${streak}</div><div class="stat-lbl">Streak</div></div>

    </div>

    ${bestComp?`<div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px;margin-bottom:12px">🏆 Best: <span style="color:#58A6FF;font-weight:600">${esc(bestComp[0])}</span> (${bestComp[1].pl>=0?"+":""}$${bestComp[1].pl.toFixed(2)} · ${bestComp[1].count} bets)</div>`:""}

    <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:7px">Recent Picks</div>

    <div style="overflow-x:auto"><table><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Match</th><th>Bet</th><th>Odds</th><th>Result</th><th>P/L</th></tr></thead><tbody>${recentRows}</tbody></table></div>

  </div>`;

}

async function genBlurb(){

  const p=window._profileBlurb;if(!p)return;

  const btn=document.getElementById("blurb-btn");if(!btn)return;

  btn.textContent="Generating…";btn.disabled=true;

  try{

    const summary=`Bettor:${p.name}. Total:${p.total}. Graded:${p.graded}. W/L/D:${p.W}/${p.L}/${p.D}. WR:${p.wr}%. P/L:$${p.pl}. AvgOdds:${p.odds}. Streak:${p.streak}.`;

    const res=await fetch("https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages",{method:"POST",headers:{"Content-Type":"application/json"},body:JSON.stringify({model:"claude-sonnet-4-6",max_tokens:200,messages:[{role:"user",content:`Write a fun, punchy 2-sentence sports betting profile blurb for a Twitch community leaderboard: ${summary}. Be energetic, like a commentator.`}]})});

    const data=await res.json();const text=data.content?.find(c=>c.type==="text")?.text||"";

    const box=document.getElementById("blurb-box");if(box){box.innerHTML=`"${esc(text)}"`;box.style.display="block";}

  }catch(e){console.error(e);}

  btn.textContent="✨ AI Blurb";btn.disabled=false;

}

let csvParsed=[];

function renderUpload(){

  if(!isL3()){document.getElementById("tab-4").innerHTML=`<div class="page"><div class="card" style="border:1px solid #E3B34144;background:#E3B34108;text-align:center;padding:28px"><div style="font-size:22px;margin-bottom:7px">🔒</div><div style="font-weight:700;color:#E3B341;margin-bottom:3px">Level 3 Access Required</div><div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px">Only Super Admins can upload CSV data.</div></div></div>`;return;}

  document.getElementById("tab-4").innerHTML=`<div class="page">

    <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px;margin-bottom:6px">📤 CSV Upload &amp; Backfill</div>

    <div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px;margin-bottom:16px">Import historical picks. Duplicates (same Twitch + bet + date) are skipped.</div>

    <div class="card" style="border-color:#58A6FF44">

      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:7px;color:#58A6FF">📋 Expected Format</div>

      <pre style="background:#0D0F14;border-radius:8px;padding:10px;font-size:10px;overflow-x:auto;line-height:1.5;margin-bottom:10px;color:#00C9A7">twitch,discord,competition,away,home,time,bet,odds,grade,date</pre>

      <button class="btn btn-ghost" style="border:1px solid #58A6FF55;color:#58A6FF;background:#58A6FF22;font-size:12px" onclick="dlTemplate()">⬇️ Download Template</button>

    </div>

    <div class="card">

      <div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:10px">Select CSV File</div>

      <label style="display:block;background:#0D0F14;border:2px dashed #21262D;border-radius:12px;padding:24px;text-align:center;cursor:pointer" onmouseover="this.style.borderColor='#00C9A7'" onmouseout="this.style.borderColor='#21262D'">

        <input type="file" id="csv-file" accept=".csv,text/csv" style="display:none" onchange="handleCSV(this)"/>

        <div style="font-size:26px;margin-bottom:5px">📂</div>

        <div id="upload-name" style="font-weight:600;margin-bottom:3px;font-size:13px">Click to select a CSV file</div>

        <div style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E">or drag and drop</div>

      </label>

    </div>

    <div id="csv-errors"></div><div id="csv-preview"></div><div id="csv-result"></div></div>`;

}

function dlTemplate(){const csv="twitch,discord,competition,away,home,time,bet,odds,grade,date\nStreamerXYZ,StreamerXYZ#1234,Premier League,Arsenal,Chelsea,15:00 BST,Arsenal Win,1.85,W,2026-01-15";const a=document.createElement("a");a.href=URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:"text/csv"}));a.download="forepack_template.csv";a.click();}

function handleCSV(input){

  const file=input.files[0];if(!file)return;

  document.getElementById("upload-name").textContent=file.name;

  const reader=new FileReader();

  reader.onload=e=>{

    const {headers,rows}=parseCSV(e.target.result);

    if(!headers.length){document.getElementById("csv-errors").innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="border-color:#F8514944"><div style="color:#F85149;font-weight:700">Could not parse CSV</div></div>`;return;}

    const FM={twitch:["twitch","twitch_name","twitchname","username","user"],discord:["discord","discord_name","discordname"],competition:["competition","comp","league","tournament"],away:["away","away_team","awayteam"],home:["home","home_team","hometeam"],gameTime:["time","gametime","game_time","kickoff"],bet:["bet","pick","selection","wager"],odds:["odds","price","decimal"],grade:["grade","result","outcome"],date:["date","submitted","created","timestamp"]};

    const norm=h=>h.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]/g,"");

    const findCol=field=>{for(const a of FM[field]){const i=headers.findIndex(h=>norm(h)===norm(a));if(i>=0)return i;}return -1;};

    const colIdx={};for(const f of Object.keys(FM))colIdx[f]=findCol(f);

    const errs=[],parsed=[];

    rows.forEach((row,i)=>{

      if(row.every(c=>!c))return;

      const get=f=>colIdx[f]>=0?(row[colIdx[f]]||"").trim():"";

      const twitch=get("twitch");if(!twitch){errs.push(`Row ${i+2}: missing Twitch name`);return;}

      const gr=get("grade").toUpperCase();const grade=["W","L","D"].includes(gr)?gr:null;

      const dateRaw=get("date");let date=new Date().toISOString();if(dateRaw){const pd=new Date(dateRaw);if(!isNaN(pd))date=pd.toISOString();}

      parsed.push({twitch,discord:get("discord"),competition:get("competition"),away:get("away"),home:get("home"),gameTime:get("gameTime"),bet:get("bet"),odds:toDecimal(get("odds"))||get("odds"),grade,date});

    });

    csvParsed=parsed;

    document.getElementById("csv-errors").innerHTML=errs.length?`<div class="card" style="border-color:#F8514944"><div style="color:#F85149;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:7px">⚠️ ${errs.length} warnings</div>${errs.slice(0,8).map(e=>`<div style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E">• ${esc(e)}</div>`).join("")}</div>`:"";

    if(!parsed.length)return;

    const pr=parsed.slice(0,10).map(r=>`<tr><td style="color:#00C9A7;font-weight:600">${esc(r.twitch)}</td><td style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px">${esc(r.discord)||"—"}</td><td style="font-size:11px">${esc(r.bet)}</td><td style="font-family:monospace;font-size:11px">${esc(r.odds)||"—"}</td><td>${gradeBadge(r.grade)}</td><td style="color:#8B949E;font-size:11px;white-space:nowrap">${r.date?new Date(r.date).toLocaleDateString():"—"}</td></tr>`).join("");

    document.getElementById("csv-preview").innerHTML=`<div class="card"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:10px"><div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:13px">Preview — ${parsed.length} rows</div><div style="font-size:11px;color:#8B949E">Showing first ${Math.min(parsed.length,10)}</div></div><button class="btn btn-primary" style="font-size:12px" onclick="doImport()">Import All →</button></div><div style="overflow-x:auto"><table><thead><tr><th>Twitch</th><th>Discord</th><th>Bet</th><th>Odds</th><th>Grade</th><th>Date</th></tr></thead><tbody>${pr}</tbody></table></div></div>`;

  };

  reader.readAsText(file);

}

function parseCSV(text){

  const lines=text.replace(/\r/g,"").split("\n").filter(l=>l.trim());

  if(lines.length<2)return{rows:[],headers:[]};

  const parseRow=line=>{const r=[];let cur="",inQ=false;for(let i=0;i<line.length;i++){const ch=line[i];if(ch==='"'&&!inQ){inQ=true;continue;}if(ch==='"'&&inQ&&line[i+1]==='"'){cur+='"';i++;continue;}if(ch==='"'&&inQ){inQ=false;continue;}if(ch===","&&!inQ){r.push(cur.trim());cur="";continue;}cur+=ch;}r.push(cur.trim());return r;};

  return{headers:parseRow(lines[0]),rows:lines.slice(1).map(parseRow)};

}

async function doImport(){

  if(!csvParsed.length)return;

  const btn=document.querySelector("#csv-preview .btn-primary");if(btn){btn.textContent="Importing…";btn.disabled=true;}

  const existing=new Set(bets.map(b=>`${b.twitch}|${b.bet}|${b.date?.slice(0,10)}`));

  const newOnes=csvParsed.filter(r=>!existing.has(`${r.twitch}|${r.bet}|${r.date?.slice(0,10)}`)).map(r=>({...r,id:uid()}));

  const skipped=csvParsed.length-newOnes.length;

  await saveBetsBulk([...bets,...newOnes]);

  csvParsed=[];document.getElementById("csv-preview").innerHTML="";

  document.getElementById("csv-result").innerHTML=`<div class="card" style="border-color:#00C9A744;background:#00C9A708;text-align:center;padding:22px"><div style="font-size:26px;margin-bottom:7px">✅</div><div style="font-weight:700;font-size:15px;color:#00C9A7;margin-bottom:3px">Import Complete!</div><div style="font-size:13px"><strong>${newOnes.length}</strong> picks added</div>${skipped>0?`<div style="color:#8B949E;font-size:12px;margin-top:3px">${skipped} duplicate${skipped!==1?"s":""} skipped</div>`:""}</div>`;

  updateHeader();if(currentTab===1)renderHistory();

}
